province_event = {
	id = DG_Zoroastrian.002
	title = DG_Zoroastrian.002.t
	desc = DG_Zoroastrian.002.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
					province_id = ROOT
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.002.warriors
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
					province_id = ROOT
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.002.farmers
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.002.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
					province_id = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = zoroastrian_great_fire_priests
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
					province_id = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
					province_id = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
			}
			add_nationalism = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
			}
			add_nationalism = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

					piety = -0.20

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
			}
			add_nationalism = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_20
			MN_HeresySpread = { typefrom = which from = MN_S0 to = 30 incr = 0.20 typeIncr = value }
			MN_Attribute_Reset = { reltype = value religion = 30 typeEffect = ENT typeStrength = value strength = 100 }
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = 2.5
				add_devotion = 5
				add_republican_tradition = 1.25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = 2
				add_devotion = 4
				add_republican_tradition = 1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = 1.5
				add_devotion = 3
				add_republican_tradition = 0.75
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = 1
				add_devotion = 2
				add_republican_tradition = 0.5
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = 0.5
				add_devotion = 1
				add_republican_tradition = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}

			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -1
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				clr_province_flag = queensland
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.023.refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				num_of_revolts = 1
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				is_at_war = yes
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					manpower_percentage = 0.75
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					manpower_percentage = 0.50
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = queensland
			}
			add_unrest = 5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				clr_province_flag = queensland
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = DG_Zoroastrian.041
	title = DG_Zoroastrian.041.t
	desc = DG_Zoroastrian.041.d
	picture = zoroastrian_priests
	trigger = {
		religion = zoroastrian
		NOT = {
			government = theocracy
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = secular_courts
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = patriarch_obedient
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_advisor = yes
				}
				random = {
					chance = 50
					set_country_flag = dispute_advisor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = dispute_advisor
					}
					num_of_merchants = 1
				}
				random = {
					chance = 30
					set_country_flag = dispute_merchant
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = dispute_advisor
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = dispute_merchant
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = dispute_noble
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.041.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 100
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 80
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 60
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					legitimacy = 40
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = -5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = -1
		}
		clr_country_flag = dispute_merchant
		clr_country_flag = dispute_noble
		clr_country_flag = dispute_advisor
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.041.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = dispute_advisor
			}
			remove_advisor = random
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = dispute_merchant
			}
			random_active_trade_node = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_trade_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							name = unhappy_merchant
						}
					}
				}
				add_trade_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					duration = 500
					power = -10
					key = unhappy_merchant
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = dispute_noble
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
				}
				add_unrest = 5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -0.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -1.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -2.5
		}
		clr_country_flag = dispute_merchant
		clr_country_flag = dispute_noble
		clr_country_flag = dispute_advisor
	}
}

	id = DG_Zoroastrian.045
	title = DG_Zoroastrian.045.t
	desc = DG_Zoroastrian.045.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					num_of_generals = 2
					NOT = {
						has_advisor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.045.general
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						num_of_generals = 2
						NOT = {
							has_advisor = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.045.advisor
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.045.dismiss
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					num_of_generals = 2
					NOT = {
						has_advisor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			kill_leader = {
				type = random
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						num_of_generals = 2
						NOT = {
							has_advisor = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			kill_advisor = random
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.045.defend
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				monthly_income = 4.2
			}
			add_years_of_income = -0.10
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = 5
			add_devotion = 10
			add_republican_tradition = 2.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = 4
			add_devotion = 8
			add_republican_tradition = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = 3
			add_devotion = 6
			add_republican_tradition = 1.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = 2
			add_devotion = 4
			add_republican_tradition = 1
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 1
			add_devotion = 2
			add_republican_tradition = 0.5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.045.ignore
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {

			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -1
		}
		add_piety = -0.20
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = impious_priests
			duration = 5000
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.047.dastur
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = caste_system_relaxed
				has_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_adm_power = -5
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = DG_Zoroastrian.049
	title = DG_Zoroastrian.049.t
	desc = DG_Zoroastrian.049.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_ruler_flag = zoroastrian_dreams_interpreted
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = bad_dream
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.049.bad_dream
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = good_dream
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.049.good_dream
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = good_dream
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = bad_dream
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.049.neutral_dream
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = good_dream
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = bad_dream
				}
				has_ruler_flag = zoroastrian_dreams
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.049.silly_dream
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.049.public
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = bad_dream
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = good_dream
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					DIP = 3
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				DIP = 5
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				DIP = 4
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		add_dip_power = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = good_dream
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					DIP = 5
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_legitimacy = 2.5
					add_devotion = 5
					add_republican_tradition = 1.25
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_legitimacy = 2
					add_devotion = 4
					add_republican_tradition = 1
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_legitimacy = 1.5
					add_devotion = 3
					add_republican_tradition = 0.75
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.60
					}
					add_legitimacy = 1
					add_devotion = 2
					add_republican_tradition = 0.5
				}
				else = {
					add_legitimacy = 0.5
					add_devotion = 1
					add_republican_tradition = 0.25
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_prestige = 5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_prestige = 4
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_prestige = 3
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.60
					}
					add_prestige = 2
				}
				else = {
					add_prestige = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					DIP = 4
				}
				random = {
					chance = 80
					if = {
						limit = {
							piety = 0.60
						}
						add_legitimacy = 2.5
						add_devotion = 5
						add_republican_tradition = 1.25
					}
					else_if = {

						}

						add_devotion = 3
						add_republican_tradition = 0.75
					}
					else_if = {

# Zoroastrian Revival # 60s and 70s (mostly one-time-only events)
#######################

country_event = {
	id = DG_Zoroastrian.061
	title = DG_Zoroastrian.061.t
	desc = DG_Zoroastrian.061.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	trigger = {
		ai = no
		AND = {
			culture_group = persian_group
		}
		check_key = { lhs = MN_36_P value = 10 } 
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = zoroastrian_sassanid_gambit
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				stability = 1
			}
			num_of_revolts = 1
			NOT = {
				legitimacy = 90
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			religion = zoroastrian
		}
		NOT = {
			government = theocracy
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20
	}
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = zoroastrian_sassanid_gambit
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.061.no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.061.yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = persian_group
				}
				religion = zoroastrian
				NOT = {
					is_core = owner
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						continent = southeast_asia
						continent = indian_continent
						continent = asia
						continent = central_asia
						continent = north_asia
					}
				}
			}
			add_core = owner
		}
		set_country_flag = voluntary_conversion
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_religion_enabled = zoroastrian
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_dangerous_religion
			Stab_Subtract1 = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_emperor_of_china = yes
				}
				add_mandate = -5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = MN_36_P value = 75 } 
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_75
			Stab_Add50Percent = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = MN_36_P value = 50 } 
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_50
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_key = { lhs = MN_36_P value = 25 } 
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_25
			Stab_Subtract1 = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_emperor_of_china = yes }
				add_mandate = -5
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = convert_population_0
			Stab_Subtract2 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.75
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_church_strong
			Stab_Subtract2 = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.50
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_piety_moderate
			Stab_Subtract1 = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_emperor_of_china = yes
				}
				add_mandate = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.25
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_church_weak
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = convert_church_insignificant
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ADM = 5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = { religion = zoroastrian }
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_strong
				Stab_Add2 = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_moderate
				Stab_Add1 = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ADM = 3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						religion = zoroastrian
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_moderate
				Stab_Add1 = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_weak
				Stab_Add50Percent = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					capital_scope = {
						religion = zoroastrian
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_weak
				Stab_Add50Percent = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_ruler_incompetent
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				advisor = theologian_CL
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_theologian
			Stab_Add50Percent = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = was_zoroastrian
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = sympathy_to_old_religion
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_previous_recent
				Stab_Add1 = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_previous_old
				Stab_Add50Percent = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = sympathy_to_old_religion
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_recent
				Stab_Add50Percent = yes
			}
		}
		change_religion = zoroastrian
		force_converted = yes
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = DG_Zoroastrian.062
	title = DG_Zoroastrian.062.t
	desc = DG_Zoroastrian.062.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		religion = zoroastrian
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = zoroastrian_avestas_restored
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = persian_group
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = DG_Zoroastrian.062.return
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.062.only
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
			}
			NOT = {
				any_known_country = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = persian_group
					}
				}
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = zoroastrian
					AND = {
						culture_group = persian_group
					}
					NOT = {
						owned_by = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							overlord_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						religion = zoroastrian
						check_key = { lhs = MN_36_P value = 20 }
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				NOT = {
					zoroastrian = 2
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = DG_Zoroastrian.063
				days = 30
				random = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.062.notonly
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
				any_known_country = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
	}
}

		set_country_flag = zoroastrianism_reformed
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
						which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = restorationist_zoroastrianism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = progressive_zoroastrianism
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.069.a
		remove_country_modifier = fragmented_scriptures
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 9
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 6
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
				duration = -1
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.6
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_observant
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = progressive_zoroastrianism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = progressive_zoroastrianism
				duration = -1
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = progressive_zoroastrianism
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.6
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_observant
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = restorationist_zoroastrianism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = restorationist_zoroastrianism
				duration = -1
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = restorationist_zoroastrianism
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.6
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_observant
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			else = {

				add_republican_tradition = -2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -3
				add_devotion = -6
				add_republican_tradition = -1.5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -2
				add_devotion = -4
				add_republican_tradition = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = -1
				add_devotion = -2
				add_republican_tradition = -0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -2.5
				add_devotion = -5
				add_republican_tradition = -1.25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -2
				add_devotion = -4
				add_republican_tradition = -1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -1.5
				add_devotion = -3
				add_republican_tradition = -0.75
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -1
				add_devotion = -2
				add_republican_tradition = -0.5
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = -0.5
				add_devotion = -1
				add_republican_tradition = -0.25
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = caste_system_harsh
		remove_country_modifier = caste_system_strict
		remove_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = caste_system_relaxed
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.50
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_pious
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_observant
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_hostile_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
					}
					patriarch_hostile_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				patriarch_hostile_observant = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
				}
				patriarch_hostile_pious = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
				}
				patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = DG_Zoroastrian.078
	title = DG_Zoroastrian.078.t
	desc = DG_Zoroastrian.078.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = zoroastrian_rivayats_collected
	}
	option = {
		name = DG_Zoroastrian.078.a
		remove_country_modifier = religious_controversy
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 9
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 6
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_rivayats
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
